 iske vajan main kami se nuksaan nahin he
 It is important to know how the rupee has weakened in the last two and a half decades and whether this weakness has caused any "catastrophe"? In the last 18 years (2000-2018), the rupee has been about 2 against the US dollar
 2 fisadi salanaa kii dar halkaa hua he
 This decline is lower than the slope from 1990 to 2000 when the rupee fell at an average rate of seven per cent
 2008 se 2018 ke bich rupaya 4
 Weakened at 9% per annum
 pichley chaar saal main anya mudraon ke mukaable rupaya sthir or thos rahaa he
 In the last two and a half decades, every two or three years, there is a cycle of fluctuations in the rupee and dollar relationship, in which the rupee is weak
 yah giravat kisi bhi tarah se na to aakasmik he or na chintajanak
 As the Indian economy became integrated with the world, the rupee has balanced itself against other currencies

 Are subject to the limit of alabatta agar karmchaaree enpies main 1
 50 lakhs
 kii buniyadi seemaa ke upar or alag se 50,000 ru
 80 can take advantage of additional deduction under CCD (1B)
 yah atirikt katautee ipief main yogadan par maujuud nahin he
 Under NPS, it is mandatory for the account holder to buy an annuity from an insurance company at the time of retirement or at the end of the extended period, at least 40% of the total amount
 baaki rakam par philhal kar dena hota he, magar bajet main baaki rakam kii bhi 40 fisadi dhanrashi ko karmukt karne or keval 20 fisadi rakam ko fouran karyogy banane kaa prastaav rakhaa gaya he
 This tax burden can also be avoided if the employee buys an annuity for 60% of the total amount
 philhal ipief kii sanchit bakaayaa rakam paripakta avadhi tak us par milane vaale byaaj sahit kar mukt he
 Withdrawal rules As far as withdrawing money from the EPF is concerned, the government tried to play with it as well and issued an order in February 2016 that the employee cannot withdraw the employer's contribution before retirement
 acha hua ki yah aadesh aakhirkaar waapas le liya gaya
 The situation at present is that the outstanding balance in EPF account can be withdrawn provided you do not transfer the outstanding amount from one employer to another
 phir bhi agar aisi dhan nikasi usee niyokta yaa kisi duusare niyokta ke tahat yogadan ke paanch saal puure hone se pehle kii gai he to nikaali gai rakam kar yogya ho jaati he or agar nikaali gai rakam 30,000 ru
 50,000, which has been increased to Rs
 50,000
 karne kaa prastaav kiya gaya he, to is par 10 fisadi kii dar se kar katautee kaa praavdhaan he
 As far as the NPS is concerned, there were no provisions to withdraw the excess money from the NPS account before the 2015 withdrawal of funds was amended
 alabatta inhen badal diya gaya or ise aanshik taur par bhavishya nidhi yojana ke anuroop banane ke liye bakaayaa rakam kii 25 fisadi rakam ko nikaalane kii chhot de di gai
 Nevertheless, the eligibility for this withdrawal is limited only to the contribution of the employee and the income arising from it
 pehle 60 saal kii umr hone par karmchaaree ke liye rakam nikaalnaa jaruri tha, lekin sanshodhit niyamon ke mutabik, karmchaaree teen saal tak nikasi ko taal saktaa he
 Also, he can choose to continue contributing till the age of 70 years
 upar kii charchaa se yah saaf ho jaataa he ki zyada tankhwaah vaale vyaktiyon ke liye enpies main ab bhi kar niyojan kaa shandaar mauka he, khaskar tab jab bajet main ipief main niyokta ke yogadan kii prastaavit seemaa lagu hone ja rahi he, jise waapas lene kaa abhi tak koi prastaav nahin he
 Who is better for either of these two depends on the individual's situation

 The country's carpet industry has also come under the grip of demonetisation
 bunakar nakadi na milane se kaam chhod rahe hai or is kaam main lage kaarobaariyon ke paas maal kii killat ke kaaran is udyog se jude sabhi log muflisi kaa dansh jhel rahe hai
 Bhadohi, Mirzapur, Panipat, etc
, which are known as the stronghold of the weaver industry, which once used to be heard by the sound of handlooms, there is silence these days
 bunakar ab duusare kaamon kii talash main apni jagahon ko chhodkar nae kaam or nai jagah kii talash main nikal rahe hai
 OP Garg, who has been associated with the carpet industry for four decades, has never faced such a crisis as it has in the last five weeks
 opi garg behad noummidi kii aawaaj main bataate hai, 'jo bunakar gaanvon main kaam karte hai unamem se zyaadaatar ke paas bank ke khate nahin hai
 Now they have left work and gone back to their respective states or those who are left are preparing to leave
 ' He explains that contractors are an important link in the flourishing of the carpet industry
 lekin ab to thekedaaron ke paas hi paisa nahin he, jisase ve bunakaron ko bhugtan nahin kar paa rahe hai
 As a result, the supply of carpets to traders has fallen by less than 50 percent
 yah sankat aise samay aayaa he jab kaaleen kaa sabase zyada niryaat hota he
 Traders fear that the supply agreements in foreign markets may not be broken
 garg bataate hai ki oktober se march tak kaaleen udyog kaa sizan hota he, in dinon videshi bazaaron main hamaare yahaan ke kalinon kii maang sabase zyaada hoti he
 Due to the demand from outside, sometimes businessmen have to make excuses to stop traffic due to cold
 tippaniyan Traders fear that if there is a delay in the supply of goods, then all contracts will be canceled in the coming days and the foreign exchange will be lost to the exporters
